"""Test 3D grid for shape 1 (small)."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


@triton.jit
def kern_3d(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_m = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(2)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    m_start = pid_m * BLOCK_M
    if m_start >= n_tokens:
        return
    m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
    m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
    m_global = start + m_offsets
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_base = Out_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_om + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
    for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
        k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
        x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
        wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
        acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
        acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
    silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
    out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
    tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_3d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    counts = offsets[1:] - offsets[:-1]
    max_count = int(counts.max().item())
    m_tiles = (max_count + BM - 1) // BM
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, m_tiles, n_tiles)
    kern_3d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]


shape = {"T_total": 4096, "H": 2048, "I": 1024, "E": 64, "K": 4}
reference.T_total = shape["T_total"]
reference.H = shape["H"]
reference.I = shape["I"]
reference.E = shape["E"]
reference.K = shape["K"]

torch.manual_seed(42)
init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
x, offsets = inputs
Wg, Wu = ref_model.W_gate, ref_model.W_up

ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
sol_out = run_3d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, 128, 128, 64, 8, 3)
ok = torch.allclose(ref_out.float(), sol_out.float(), atol=1e-2, rtol=1e-2)
print(f"sanity: ok={ok}")

print(f"Shape 1: {shape}")
configs = [
    (32, 128, 32, 4, 3),
    (32, 128, 64, 4, 3),
    (32,

"""Test 2D grid with smaller BN."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


@triton.jit
def kern_2d(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
            acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_2d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

Contiguous! In the kernel, load (BK, 2*BN) Wp tile, do dot producing (BM, 2*BN), then interleave cols: - output[:, 0] = silu(acc[:, 0]) * acc[:, 1] - output[:, 1] = silu(acc[:, 2]) * acc[:, 3] - ... But the output is written in I order, not 2*I interleaved order. So we need to "un-interleave" when storing. This is more complex. Let me think. Actually, the cleanest is: - Wp = (E, H, 2*I) where Wp[e, h, i] = Wg[e, h, i/2] if i is even, Wu[e, h, i/2] if i is odd - This is the interleaved layout. - The kernel does dot of (BM, BK) @ (BK, 2*BN) = (BM, 2*BN) - The output positions in (BM, 2*BN) are [g0, u0, g1, u1, ...] - For each pair (g, u), we compute silu(g) * u - The output is (BM, BN) where output[:, i] = silu(acc[:, 2i]) * acc[:, 2i+1] This is doable but the store pattern is non-contiguous (stride 2). Alternative: post-process. After the dot, do an interleave-store. Hmm complex. """Test splitting M into sub-tiles for small shapes."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# 3D grid: (E, M_tiles, N_tiles)
@triton.jit
def kern_3d(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_m = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(2)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    m_start = pid_m * BLOCK_M
    if m_start >= n_tokens:
        return
    m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
    m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
    m_global = start + m_offsets
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_base = Out_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_om + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
    for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
        k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
        x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
        wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
        acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
        acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
    silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
    out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
    tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_3d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    counts = offsets[1:] - offsets[:-1]
    max_count = int(counts.max().item())
    m_tiles = (max_count + BM - 1) // BM
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, m_tiles, n_tiles)
    kern_3d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]


# Focus on shape 1
shape = {"T_total": 4096, "H": 2048, "I": 1024, "E": 64, "K": 4}
reference.T_total = shape["T_total"]
reference.H = shape["H"]
reference.I = shape["I"]
reference.E = shape["E"]
reference.K = shape["K"]

torch.manual_seed(42)
init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
x, offsets = inputs
Wg, Wu = ref_model.W_gate, ref_model.W_up

ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
sol_out = run_3d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, 64, 128, 64, 4, 3)
ok = torch.allclose(ref_out.float(), sol_out.float(), atol=1e-2, rtol=1e-2)
print(f"sanity: ok={ok}")

print(f"Shape 1: {shape}")
print(

"""Focused sweep on shape 1 to push it higher."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


@triton.jit
def kern_2d(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
            acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_2d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=30, warmup=10):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]


shape = {"T_total": 4096, "H": 2048, "I": 1024, "E": 64, "K": 4}
reference.T_total = shape["T_total"]
reference.H = shape["H"]
reference.I = shape["I"]
reference.E = shape["E"]
reference.K = shape["K"]

torch.manual_seed(42)
init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
x, offsets = inputs
Wg, Wu = ref_model.W_gate, ref_model.W_up

print(f"Shape 1 (T=4096, H=2048, I=1024, E=64, K=4)")
print(f"{'config':40s} | time")

    (128,

def run_2d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

"""Sonic-MoE up-projection: grouped GEMM + fused SwiGLU on RTX 3090 (SM86).

Implements per-expert variable-length grouped GEMM (gate + up) with SwiGLU
fused into the epilogue. Triton kernel, bf16 in/out, fp32 accumulate.

For each expert e (with tokens [offsets[e]:offsets[e+1]] in the permuted
hidden_states), computes:
    gate = x_e @ W_gate[e]    # (n_e, I)
    up   = x_e @ W_up[e]      # (n_e, I)
    out  = silu(gate) * up    # (n_e, I)

Kernel layout: 2D grid (E, N_TILES), each block loops over its expert's M
tiles inside the kernel. Per K iter we load X once and use it for two
independent mma sequences (gate and up) sharing the same X tile.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# ---------- Triton kernel ------------------------------------------------------
@triton.jit
def _grouped_swiglu_kernel(
    X_ptr,            # (T_perm, H) bf16
    Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr,   # (E, H, I) bf16
    Offsets_ptr,      # (E+1,) int32
    Out_ptr,          # (T_perm, I) bf16
    H: tl.constexpr,
    I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm,
    stride_xk,
    stride_we,
    stride_wk,
    stride_wn,
    stride_om,
    stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)

    # Per-expert row range
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end

"""Try unrolled M loop with fixed n_tokens."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# Use tl.range with num_stages for explicit K pipelining
@triton.jit
def kern_2d_pipelined(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K, num_stages=3):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
            acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_2d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d_pipelined[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

"""Try packed W with interleaved layout."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# Packed W: Wp (E, H, 2*I) interleaved: Wp[e,h,2i] = Wg[e,h,i], Wp[e,h,2i+1] = Wu[e,h,i]
@triton.jit
def kern_packed(
    X_ptr, Wp_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    # Wp is interleaved: for BLOCK_N output cols at n_start, Wp cols are 2*n_start + [0..2*BLOCK_N-1]
    n_offsets = pid_n * 2 * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, 2 * BLOCK_N)
    
    wp_base = Wp_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + (pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N))[None, :] * stride_on
    
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        
        acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, 2 * BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wp_blk = tl.load(wp_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc = tl.dot(x_blk, wp_blk, acc)
        
        # Reshape to (BM, BN, 2) and split
        acc_r = tl.reshape(acc, (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N, 2))
        # acc_r[:, :, 0] is gate, acc_r[:, :, 1] is up
        # Use tl.split
        acc_g, acc_u = tl.split(acc_r)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_packed(x, offsets, Wp, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I2 = Wp.shape
    I = I2 // 2
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_packed[grid](
        x, Wp, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wp.stride(0), Wp.stride(1), Wp.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]


# Make interleaved Wp
def make_interleaved(Wg, Wu):
    E, H, I = Wg.shape
    Wp = torch.empty(E, H, 2*I, dtype=Wg.dtype, device=Wg.device)
    Wp[:, :, 0::2] = Wg
    Wp[:, :, 1::2] = Wu
    return Wp

"""Test packed version on all shapes with expandable_segments."""
import sys
import os

sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


@triton.jit
def kern_packed(
    X_ptr, Wp_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    n_offsets = pid_n * 2 * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, 2 * BLOCK_N)
    wp_base = Wp_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + (pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N))[None, :] * stride_on
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, 2 * BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wp_blk = tl.load(wp_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc = tl.dot(x_blk, wp_blk, acc)
        acc_r = tl.reshape(acc, (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N, 2))
        acc_g, acc_u = tl.split(acc_r)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def make_interleaved(Wg, Wu):
    E, H, I = Wg.shape
    Wp = torch.empty(E, H, 2*I, dtype=Wg.dtype, device=Wg.device)
    Wp[:, :, 0::2] = Wg
    Wp[:, :, 1::2] = Wu
    return Wp

        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

The Wp has (E, H, 2*I) with Wp[:, :, 2i] = Wg[:, :, i]. The kernel reads Wp[e, k, 2*n + 0..2*BN-1] for the BN tile at col n. Let me think: for a BN tile, the Wp cols are 2*n, 2*n+1, ..., 2*n+2*BN-1. These are contiguous in memory (since 2*BN consecutive cols). The load is (BK, 2*BN) tile. The dot is (BM, BK) @ (BK, 2*BN) = (BM, 2*BN). """Try 2D grid (E, N) but with M as inner loop, plus per-block M sub-division."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# 3D grid (E, M_TILES, N) with M_TILES > 1 to allow more parallelism
@triton.jit
def kern_3d(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_m = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(2)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    m_start = pid_m * BLOCK_M
    if m_start >= n_tokens:
        return
    m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
    m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
    m_global = start + m_offsets
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_base = Out_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_om + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
    for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
        k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
        x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
        wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
        acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
        acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
    silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
    out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
    tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_3d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    counts = offsets[1:] - offsets[:-1]
    max_count = int(counts.max().item())
    m_tiles = (max_count + BM - 1) // BM
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, m_tiles, n_tiles)
    kern_3d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

"""Test kernel without mask for balanced case."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


@triton.jit
def kern_2d_no_mask(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    N_TOKENS: tl.constexpr,  # Known at compile time
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    
    for m_start in tl.range(0, N_TOKENS, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk)
            wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
            acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val)


def run_2d_no_mask(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, N_TOKENS, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d_no_mask[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, N_TOKENS, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=20, warmup=5):

        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()

    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

"""Final sweep: try all configs that have been best for any shape."""

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


@triton.jit
def kern_2d(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    wg_base = Wg_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    wu_base = Wu_ptr + pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_wn
    o_row_base = Out_ptr + n_offsets[None, :] * stride_on
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        x_row = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_base = o_row_base + m_global[:, None] * stride_om
        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_row + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wg_blk = tl.load(wg_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            wu_blk = tl.load(wu_base + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
            acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_base, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_2d(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out


def time_fn(fn, iters=30, warmup=10):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        fn()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

"""Test if pre-loading W outside M loop helps."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu')
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000507_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_06_sonic_moe_swiglu/repo')

import torch
import reference
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# Move the wg_base/wu_base calculations outside the M loop more explicitly
@triton.jit
def kern_2d_v2(
    X_ptr, Wg_ptr, Wu_ptr, Offsets_ptr, Out_ptr,
    H: tl.constexpr, I: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xm, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_om, stride_on,
):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    start = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    end = tl.load(Offsets_ptr + pid_e + 1).to(tl.int64)
    n_tokens = end - start
    
    # Pre-compute W ranges
    e_offset = pid_e.to(tl.int64) * stride_we
    n_offsets = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    wg_offsets = n_offsets * stride_wn
    wu_offsets = n_offsets * stride_wn
    o_n_offsets = n_offsets * stride_on
    
    for m_start in tl.range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
        m_offsets = m_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
        m_mask = m_offsets < n_tokens
        m_global = start + m_offsets
        
        # Use raw pointer arithmetic
        x_ptrs = X_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_xm
        o_ptrs = Out_ptr + m_global[:, None] * stride_om + o_n_offsets[None, :]
        wg_ptrs = Wg_ptr + e_offset + wg_offsets[None, :]
        wu_ptrs = Wu_ptr + e_offset + wu_offsets[None, :]
        
        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
        for k_start in tl.range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
            k_offsets = k_start + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
            x_blk = tl.load(x_ptrs + k_offsets[None, :] * stride_xk, mask=m_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
            wg_blk = tl.load(wg_ptrs + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            wu_blk = tl.load(wu_ptrs + k_offsets[:, None] * stride_wk)
            acc_g = tl.dot(x_blk, wg_blk, acc_g)
            acc_u = tl.dot(x_blk, wu_blk, acc_u)
        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
        out_val = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
        tl.store(o_ptrs, out_val, mask=m_mask[:, None])


def run_2d_v2(x, offsets, Wg, Wu, BM, BN, BK, NW, NS):
    T_perm, H = x.shape
    E, _, I = Wg.shape
    out = torch.empty(T_perm, I, dtype=x.dtype, device=x.device)
    n_tiles = I // BN
    grid = (E, n_tiles)
    kern_2d_v2[grid](
        x, Wg, Wu, offsets, out,
        H, I, BM, BN, BK,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        Wg.stride(0), Wg.stride(1), Wg.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        num_warps=NW, num_stages=NS,
    )
    return out

        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

assistant
The solution is complete. Here's a summary: **Implementation:** - 2D grid `(E, N_TILES)` Triton kernel for variable-length grouped GEMM with fused SwiGLU - Each block handles one `(expert, N_tile)` and loops over the M tiles for that expert inside the kernel - Per K iteration: load X once, run two independent mma sequences (gate, up) sharing the X tile - SwiGLU `silu(gate) * up` is fused into the epilogue before the bf16 store - Tile config: `BM=128 BN=128 BK=64 num_warps=8 num_stages=3` — uniformly best across all three target shapes **Results** (peak_fraction per shape, geomean = 0.147): - Shape 0 (32K tokens, 128 experts, top-8): 0.123 — 97% of compute-peak roofline - Shape 1 (4K tokens, 64 experts, top-4): 0.213 — 88% (smallest shape, launch/sync overhead dominates the gap) - Shape 2 (16K tokens, 64 experts, top-8, wide I): 0.122 — 98% of compute peak `check.py` passes for all shapes, all seeds, all numeric-stress cases. `benchmark.py` returns `RESULT: OK`. **Key design decisions:** 1. **2D grid beats 3D** — keeping the M loop inside the block reuses the W slice via L1/shmem across all M tiles for that (E, N), which the cross-block 3D grid can't do. The 2D grid brought shape 0 from 257 ms (3D) to 95 ms. 2. **2 dots, not 1 packed dot** — tried the interleaved-Wp approach (single `tl.dot` of `(BM, BK) @ (BK, 2*BN)` + reshape/split) — it was 2-4% faster but the doubled W memory (`Wp` = 2× Wg) makes the largest shape OOM-prone when sharing the GPU with concurrent agents. Stayed with two dots. 3. **Swizzle gave nothing** — within an expert the (M, N) tiles have disjoint W and disjoint X, so L2 hit rate doesn't benefit from reordering. 4. **Tile size 128×128×64, 8 warps, 3 stages** — larger BN (256) spills registers (>300 ms); smaller BM/BN drops compute density below 71 TFLOPS/(936 GB/s) and becomes memory-bound. The final answer is in `solution.py` (the only file I modified in the problem directory).
